✔RQ.SRS-033.ClickHouse.ExtractKeyValuePairs.Function

ClickHouse SHALL support extractKeyValuePairs function that SHALL have the following syntax:

extractKeyValuePairs(<column_name>|<constant>|<function_return_value>|<alias>[, key_value_pair_delimiter[, pair_delimiters[, quoting_character]]]])

For example,

Insert into the table parsed key-values from another table

INSERT INTO table_2 SELECT extractKeyValuePairs(x) FROM table_1;

The function SHALL return a map object containing all recognized parsed keys and values.

{'key': 'value', ...}

✔RQ.SRS-033.ClickHouse.ExtractKeyValuePairs.Key.Format

ClickHouse's extractKeyValuePairs function SHALL recognize the key in the input string if it satisfies the following conditions:

  • Key can't contain symbols that defined in parameters.
  • Key can't be an empty string.
  • If a key is enclosed, value can contain any symbols.
  • If extractKeyValuePairsWithEscaping is used, key shall accept control symbols.

✔RQ.SRS-033.ClickHouse.ExtractKeyValuePairs.Parameters.QuotingCharacter.Format

ClickHouse's extractKeyValuePairs function SHALL return an error if quoting_character parameter specified with non-string value or string value with more than one symbol.

OK249ms/key value/parameters formats/quoting character format
    Scenario quoting character format
      Check that `quoting_character` can be specified only with one symbol.
      Given I specify supported and unsupported parameters
      OK
      When I check ClickHouse supports properly specified `quoting_character` parameter
      OK
        By executing command
          echo -e "SELECT extractKeyValuePairs('a:a', ':', ',', '1')" | clickhouse client -n 2>&1
        OK
        Then check if output has exception
        OK
        By executing command
          echo -e "SELECT extractKeyValuePairs('a:a', ':', ',', 'q')" | clickhouse client -n 2>&1
        OK
        Then check if output has exception
        OK
      When I check ClickHouse returns an error if `quoting_character` specified wrong
      OK
        By executing command
          echo -e "SELECT extractKeyValuePairs('a:a', ':', ',', 'grkgork')" | clickhouse client -n 2>&1
        OK
        By executing command
          echo -e "SELECT extractKeyValuePairs('a:a', ':', ',', 1203)" | clickhouse client -n 2>&1
        OK
        By executing command
          echo -e "SELECT extractKeyValuePairs('a:a', ':', ',', [])" | clickhouse client -n 2>&1
        OK
        By executing command
          echo -e "SELECT extractKeyValuePairs('a:a', ':', ',', [100])" | clickhouse client -n 2>&1
        OK
    OK
✔RQ.SRS-033.ClickHouse.ExtractKeyValuePairs.Parameters.ExtractKeyValuePairsWithEscaping

ClickHouse SHALL support extractKeyValuePairsWithEscaping function that SHALL allow using control symbols in keys and values and allow specifying symbols in hexadecimal format.

For example:

SELECT extractKeyValuePairsWithEscaping('a:\\x0A', ':', ',', '\"')

SHALL return

{'a':' '}

✔RQ.SRS-033.ClickHouse.ExtractKeyValuePairs.Parameters.SpecialCharactersConflict

ClickHouse's extractKeyValuePairs function SHALL return an error if either key_value_pair_delimiter, pair_delimiter, or quoting_character parameters use the same symbol.

For example:

SELECT extractKeyValuePairs('a=a', '=', '=', '=')

OK2s 129ms/key value/special symbols conflict
  Feature special symbols conflict
    Check that ClickHouse's extractKeyValuePairs function returns an error if
    either `key_value_pair_delimiter`, `pair_delimiter`, or `quoting_character`
    parameters use the same symbol.
    Feature key_value_pair_delimiter and pair_delimiters
    OK
      Scenario special symbols conflict

        either `key_value_pair_delimiter`, `pair_delimiter`, or `quoting_character`
